PROMPT:

            Compressor: [REDACTED] (ideally) and such that you (llama-3.1-8b-instant) can reconstruct the intention of the human who wrote text as close as possible to the original intention. This is for yourself. It does not need to be human readable or understandable. Abuse of language mixing, abbreviations, symbols (unicode and emoji), or any other encodings or internal representations is all permissible, as long as it, if pasted in a new inference cycle, will yield near-identical results as the original text:
            The personal income of Joe Biden is
            

ANSWER:
```python
# Original Text: The personal income of Joe Biden is
# Compressing text into a compact, machine-readable format

import re
import base64

# Remove unnecessary characters and convert to lower case
text = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]', '', "The personal income of Joe Biden is").lower()

# Tokenize text into individual words
words = text.split()

# Represent each word as a numerical index
word_indices = [i for i in range(len(words))]

# Compress word indices using base64 encoding
compressed_indices = base64.b64encode(str(word_indices).encode()).decode()

# Compress the original text using base64 encoding
compressed_text = base64.b64encode(text.encode()).decode()

# Combine compressed text and indices into a single string
compressed_output = f"{compressed_text},{compressed_indices}"

print(compressed_output)
```
